Domestic News

He Chengjun Returns to Hankou

Makes a Statement to Reporters

Hankou Correspondence: He Chengjun, acting commander of the Wuhan Xingying, attended the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee in Nanjing. After the meeting, he went to Shanghai for medical treatment on the 22nd due to stomach problems. Believing that government affairs and bandit suppression matters were important, he took a postal flight from Shanghai to Hankou at 7:00 AM on the 25th. The Xingying and the provincial government had already received He's telegram, notifying various agencies and groups to prepare a welcome. Those who went to Wangjiadun Airport to meet him on that day included Xu Yuanquan, commander of the 16th Route; Xia Douyin, commander of the 21st Route; Chen Guangzu, chief of staff of the Xingying; Wu Xingya, acting chairman of the provincial government; Fang Dazhi, director of the Construction Department; Huang Jianzhong, director of the Education Department; Committee members Peng Jieshi, Xiong Bingkun, and Xie Lu; Secretary-General Hua Jueming; Liu Wendao, mayor of Hankou; and representatives from various agencies, groups, and schools. The 1st Battalion of the 1st Supplementary Regiment of the 48th Division and the Security Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau were responsible for perimeter security. At 3:10 PM, the China Airlines postal flight arrived at the airport. Military music played loudly and cheers rang out. After He got off the plane, he greeted the welcomers one by one and then, along with Fan Shisheng, commander of the 51st Division, and Xu Langxi, chief of staff of the 3rd Army, got into cars and returned to their private residences to rest. At 4:00 PM, He went to the headquarters of the 3rd Army and talked with the two commanders Xu and Xia and Acting Chairman Wu and Mayor Liu about the military and political situation after he left Hankou. After about ten minutes, he met with reporters and made the following statement: "I went to Nanjing this time to attend the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee. Because Vice Commander Zhang was coming to Nanjing, I went a day or two earlier to prepare for the welcome and reception. After the meeting, I took the opportunity to go to Shanghai for treatment due to illness. I was only able to return to Hankou today. The results of the Fourth Plenary Session were excellent. All the resolutions made, which are related to long-term plans, have been handed over to the responsible agencies for handling. As for the post-war affairs in the north, General Chiang Kai-shek and Vice Commander Zhang are currently discussing them in Nanjing and have come to a proper solution. When I left Nanjing, the Taiyuan Garrison Commander Rong Honglu came to Nanjing to pay respects to the Commander-in-Chief and ask for instructions. He said that Yan and Feng have decided to go abroad within days, and the northwestern provinces are completely listening to the orders of the Central Government. Vice Commander Zhang is now stopping over in Shanghai and will return north soon to preside over everything. General Chiang Kai-shek will come to Hankou after Vice Commander Zhang goes north to inspect the bandit situation in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces, and to supervise and order the troops to encircle and suppress them according to the plan. Believing that the bandits will be cleared within the scheduled time." (25th)

Repeated Negotiations Regarding the "Wanshin" Steamer Incident

The Hankow Municipal Government Sends Another Letter to the Japanese Consul

Hankow Dispatch: The case of the Japanese naval vessel colliding with and sinking the "Wanshin" steamer has been repeatedly negotiated by the Municipal Government without result. Instead, the Japanese Consul has presented a defense to the Municipal Government, making many accusations. The Municipal Government, on the 25th, sent another letter to the Japanese Consul, refuting each point of the defense and requesting that the previous letter regarding compensation for losses be reviewed. The Director of the Health Bureau, Li Boren, was also sent in person to negotiate. The original letter is excerpted below:

"Regarding your esteemed letter of October 30th concerning the collision and sinking of the "Wanshin" merchant steamer by your country's naval vessel, in which you made two accusations and forwarded a rebuttal from the commander of the "Shibuya Hirato" warship for our review, requesting that the shipping company "Xinghan," the owner of the ship, acknowledge the conditions previously proposed by the navy, we have carefully reviewed the same. Upon investigation, the two accusations in the letter are completely untrue, and the "Shibuya" commander's rebuttal also contains many contradictions and misunderstandings. We hereby refute them one by one as follows:

(1) Regarding the first point, which vaguely states that there was no instance of passengers being prevented from disembarking with guns after the "Hanhua" (i.e., "Wanxin") incident, only that a staff officer belonging to the headquarters within the "Ataka" warship used his bare hands to prevent everyone from disembarking at once. Upon investigation, after the "Hanhua" was damaged in the collision, water poured in profusely. The ship's chief mate, in order to protect the lives of all passengers, urgently steered the ship close to shore. In this critical moment of life and death, anyone with a modicum of humanity would be trying to rescue them, how could they be prevented? Even if, as stated in the letter, the method of prevention was by hand and not by gun, the effect of not allowing passengers to disembark would be no different than a means of causing death. If it was considered there was no danger, why prevent it? At the time, the "Hanhua" sounded its whistle first, and the passengers cried for help after, the dangerous situation was known to all. The staff officer still believed that the collision was minimal and would not cause a critical event, how ignorant of the situation could they be? Even more strange is that the original letter speculates that the cause of the "Hanhua" sinking did not occur before the passengers disembarked, but after. We wonder on what basis is this claimed? In ordinary theory, once the passengers have disembarked, the load is empty and the draft is very shallow, the ship is already in a safe state, how could the cause of sinking occur? This kind of cause was definitely before the passengers disembarked, there is no doubt about that.

(2) Regarding the second point, which states that the "Hanhua" captain's attitude at the time of the incident was puzzling. The ship sailed in the naval machinery bridge area, where ordinary ships are not allowed to enter or exit, after colliding with the "Hinode Maru." It then continued to dock at the pier, allowing passengers to disembark, and then moved the machinery, colliding with the wooden bridge connecting the machinery bridge to the shore, breaking four bridge timbers, before moving close to the shore and sinking. Upon investigation, if the "Hanhua" had only suffered a minor collision and was not far from the company's pier, there would have been no difficulty in sailing to its own pier for berthing. Why would it need to dock at the naval pier? Even if it had forcibly entered, the dozens of people on board, not having reached their destination (i.e., the company's pier), would certainly not be willing to disembark. Furthermore, let's concede for a moment: if, as stated in the letter, the machinery was started after the passengers disembarked and the machinery bridge was broken, then the "Hanhua's" serious damage must have been to the bow and definitely not to the midships. Moreover, if the ship had no insurance, what could be the "ulterior motive" in seeking compensation?

As for the points in the "Shibuya" commander's rebuttal: (1) He states that it is difficult to accept that the "Wanxin" captain stopped the engine and reversed before the collision. He claims that the "Wanxin's" forward momentum was naturally very great at the time of the collision, and that even after the collision, the "Wanxin" would have reached the naval pontoon by its own inertia. Upon investigation, after the "Wanxin" sounded its whistle and reversed, the Public Security Bureau conducted investigations from all sides, and the testimonies were consistent. Even Consul Tanaka stated that it was indeed the case. Now the letter states that even if stopping the engine and reversing were true, it must have been after the collision and did not raise any sufficient evidence and concrete reasons, which is unavoidable arbitrary. (2) He states that the Wuchang Customs surveyor mistakenly identified the circumstances of the collision as being the same as previously described. He claims. The surveyor, Mr. Jin's original report stated that he asked Wuchang Customs' Mr. Mao, and that colleague and himself were viewing from the Jiang An (riverbank) that afternoon. He did not point out where the office building was. Now the letter insists that he was in front of the office and could not see the situation of the collision, which is a mistake. (3) He states that when the surveyor, Mr. Jin met with Consul Tanaka, they thought that the damaged part of the right midship of the Japanese "Hinode Maru" was damaged a long time ago, and was not caused by the present case. He states that the misjudgment was astonishing. Upon investigation, Mr. Jin's inspection was only five days after the incident. It is not difficult to tell at a glance that it was a new wound. If the surveyor had falsely claimed that the old wounds were new wounds, Consul Tanaka should have immediately declared it at the time and requested an assessment. Since there was no such statement at the time, it is sufficient to show that Mr. Jin determined that the wound on the midship of the right side of the Japanese warship must be a long time ago, which is reality. (4) He states that the claim of whether the "Wanxin" reversed is questionable, and that the statements of other parties involved are mostly misunderstandings of the facts of the case and are not sufficient to be used as evidence. He also claims that the ship "Wanxin" had no reason to enter the bay, but unexpectedly entered improperly, causing the accident. Upon investigation, cases rely on evidence. The statements of all parties involved in this case are consistent, which is sufficient to become an ironclad case. The captain of the warship simply denied everything and claimed that it was a misunderstanding and insufficient to be used as evidence. The argument is particularly unfair. It also said before that the ship had no reason to enter the bay, but unexpectedly entered improperly, and then said that it was a common thing according to shipping conventions, which seems contradictory. (5) He states that Mr. Jin's report that the Japanese warship could not stop the machinery in a place where the water flow is rapid more than 20 zhang away is a misunderstanding, and he exposes his ignorance. Upon investigation, Mr. Jin reported that the Japanese warship could not stop the machinery in a place where the water flow is rapid more than 20 zhang away, which was actually to refute Consul Tanaka's claim that the naval vessel stopped the machinery and waited. It was not that the Japanese warship stopped the machinery at that place. The misunderstanding is actually not the fault of Mr. Jin. (6) He states that at the time of the collision, the "Wanxin" had a fast speed, and it was not pushed by the water flow, and it was able to reach the bridge before the "Hinode Maru." Upon investigation, the "Wanxin" was going up the river and suddenly encountered the Japanese warship rushing across. At that time, it sounded its whistle and retreated, which is an undeniable fact. Also, after being hit, the water flow pressed and rushed, which is also true. Because it was not pushed by the water flow, it went to the shore, and it would not have resulted in sinking. After being damaged, it was in great danger. If it was not driven urgently, the lives of the entire ship would not be guaranteed. Therefore, the Japanese warship reached the bridge first.

Now, the last two points of the letter are refuted in detail: (1) The "Wanxin" avoided the usual upstream route and even entered the inner side of the naval pier. Upon investigation, the route taken by the "Wanxin" was directly to the Xianghekou. At that time, the reason why it entered the naval pier was that it was hit by the Japanese warship and pushed by the water flow. In order to protect the lives of the entire ship, it had to do so. If it had avoided the usual route for no reason and sailed into the naval pier, not only would it not have been allowed by the naval authorities, but the entire ship's passengers would have been criticized for stopping before reaching their destination, which is obvious. (2) The "Wanxin" captain's error in steering to avoid the collision caused him to overtake the "Hinode Maru," which had already stopped its engine. Upon investigation, when the "Wanxin" sailed to the river surface of the Japanese concession, the Japanese warship rushed across. The captain of the ship sounded its whistle, stopped the engine, and retreated. His method of avoidance was without error. To say that he overtook the "Hinode Maru," which had already stopped its engine, is completely inconsistent with the facts and is also unreasonable. Knowing that the Japanese warship was an iron warship, how could he use an egg to hit a stone and bring about his own demise?

In conclusion, the "Wanxin" was sunk due to no fault of its own, and its chief mate, Dong Changsheng, was also wrongfully detained for a week. The extent of the losses is unspeakable. The government negotiated based on reason last time, hoping to calm things down and bring them to an early conclusion. However, the reply denies everything and instead demands that we acknowledge the conditions previously proposed, which is unreasonable and unfair. In addition to sending Director Li Boren to negotiate further, and consulting the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for the record, we hereby respond with a rebuttal based on reason. Please review the previous letter regarding compensation for losses and we hope to hear back. (November 25th)

Japan's Manchurian and Mongolian Railway Policy

Japanese Admit They Have Entered an Era of Suffering

Criticizing the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for Lacking Thorough Countermeasures

Shenyang Dispatch: Japan's ambition to invade Manchuria and Mongolia is obvious and well known to all Chinese people. Recently, the Japanese newspaper "Fengtian Daily News" published an article by a Japanese named Takeuchisei, titled "Our Country's Manchurian and Mongolian Policy Has Fallen into a Head-on Crisis," which is tantamount to revealing its true colors. The original text is as follows:

"Since the Chinese side built the Datong Line in the fourteenth year of Taisho, our country's (referring to Japan) Manchurian and Mongolian policy has undergone a change and entered an era of suffering. Later, the former president of the South Manchuria Railway, Yamamoto, made a false agreement with Zhang Zuolin for five new Manchurian and Mongolian railways, and the establishment of the Great Liang Railway agreement by Chairman Ji, which temporarily eased the frown. However, the sudden death of Zhang Zuolin in the June 4th Incident in the third year of Showa further deteriorated the situation. Recently, the Chinese side has completely disregarded our country's vested rights and protests under the treaty, and built railways to compete with the South Manchuria Railway. Because of the extension of the diplomatic power of the National Government to the three eastern provinces, coupled with Zhang Xueliang's avoidance policy, local solutions have become difficult, and the South Manchuria Railway's era of monopoly over the Manchurian and Mongolian railways has been obviously shaken. However, with the sharp decline in the world's silver price this spring, the South Manchuria Railway, which uses the gold standard, is under a major threat in the competition for freight transportation compared to the Chinese railways, which use the silver standard. Moreover, the long-feared formidable enemy of Dalian Port, namely the construction of Huludao Port, actually started construction in July of this year. The Chinese side's attitude of challenging us has become openly expressed, and it is also the vanguard of the emergence of international threats. Recently, the authorities of the four eastern provinces and the German consortium are starting to implement a large loan of 50 million yuan for the purpose of building the three major trunk lines of Manchuria and Mongolia, which is another new international threat. As such, the South Manchuria Railway policy, which is the pivot of our country's Manchurian and Mongolian policy, is now facing a crisis of internal and external flaws and is in a very difficult situation.

Based on the above reasons, the South Manchuria Railway, which is the main body of the Manchurian and Mongolian policy, has experienced a large reduction in railway revenue of more than 10 million yuan in the past six months. The budget for this year is becoming more and more troublesome. At first, it was thought that the estimated reduction would be 10%, but after substantive investigation, it is feared that it will reach the difficult situation of a reduction of 70% or 80%. However, at this time, when observing the overall situation, the focus of this problem is obvious, that is, whether the construction of independent railways by the Great Chinese side will be thoroughly implemented, what will be the international situation, and the relationship between Chinese unification and the four eastern provinces. This will be the turning point to determine the expansion and contraction of our country's rights in Manchuria and Mongolia. Furthermore, to what extent can the Manchurian and Mongolian railway policy be implemented, or is it impossible? Regarding this point, it is now a major issue, and what will be of major importance to our country's Manchurian and Mongolian railway policy in the future? (1) The Chinese side is currently resolutely taking intentional resistance actions against our country. (A) The Qiyao, Tao'ang, Siping-Tao'ang, Datong, and Beining railways. (B) The direct connection of the two major Chinese trunk lines, the Jihai, Shenhai, and Beining railways. (2) Whether the three major trunk lines stipulated in the loan of 50 million yuan allowed by the German consortium mentioned above will be built, and how the two major Chinese trunk line railways will be directly connected.

The Japanese side believes that the most deeply concerned matter is when the Shenhai Road on the Chinese side was completed. When the railway was to be connected with the Beining Railway, the South Manchuria Railway on the Japanese side resolutely rejected its connection with the reason of six points, because it had major relations. However, the Chinese side recently took advantage of the weakness of the Japanese side and implemented it with only a unilateral notification to the South Manchuria Railway. The direct connection of freight between the Tao'ang, Siping-Tao'ang, Datong, and Beining railways has been realized. The direct connection of the Jihai, Shenhai, and Beining railways was also implemented on October 10th. At present, direct transportation of passengers has started twice a day, and there is also a form of direct transportation of goods. As for the loan from Germany, (1) the construction of the Tongliao-Taonan line via Qiqihar to Daheihe line, (2) the construction of the line from Jilin via Yilan, Fujin, Tongjiang to Suiyuan line, (3) The construction of the line from Huludao via Linghe to Kulun in Outer Mongolia are the three major trunk lines. Whether they will be built will not only have a great impact on the Manchurian and Mongolian policy, but also has completed the railway trunk line surrounding the South Manchuria Railway, which will inevitably have a profound impact on the South Manchuria Railway.

The above two matters not only cause a fatal blow to the railway policy that forms the cornerstone of the Manchurian and Mongolian policy, but also become a major issue concerning the interests and prestige of the South Manchuria Railway and our country. Recently, discerning people's nerves have been stimulated by this, and they feel that the South Manchuria Railway is very different from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, which is indecisive. Why don't they thoroughly study countermeasures? It is a matter of even greater concern." (21st)

Anniversary Commemoration of the Defense Against Russia in Heilongjiang Province

Unveiling Ceremony Held for the Tombstones of Fallen Soldiers

The 17th Brigade Stationed in the Province Holds a Public Memorial Service at the Martyrs' Shrine

The Family of Han Guangdi Receives an Additional 30,000 Yuan in Compensation

Heilongjiang Dispatch: Last year, during the Northeast's defense against Russia, the soldiers of the 15th and 17th brigades fought and defended in Zhalainuo'er and Manchuria, etc. Eventually, due to exhaustion of ammunition and lack of reinforcements, Zhalainuo'er and Manzhouli were successively captured. The loss of Zhalainuo'er was particularly tragic, with the commander of the 17th Brigade, Han Guangdi, the regimental commanders Lin Xuanqing and Zhang Xiaoying, and dozens of other officers and men perishing in the battle. The Northeast authorities have already had the deceased generals and soldiers enshrined in

Page 8

the provincial shrine to commend their loyalty and valor. As for the remains of all officers and soldiers, the government built public cemeteries in Zhalainuo'er and Manzhouli this spring, buried them separately, and erected steles to commemorate them permanently and show them to the country. After the completion of the work, the Commander of the Hulunbuir Garrison, Su Bingwen, submitted a report to Commander Wan, who decided to hold the unveiling ceremony of the tombstone on November 17th of this year, the anniversary of the defense against Russia. Yesterday, the 17th, was the date for the unveiling ceremony. Mr. Su invited people from all walks of life in the Northeast to participate in the ceremony in advance, and also held a memorial service for the fallen soldiers of the 15th and 17th brigades who died in the defense against Russia. On this day, the Railway Bureau specially opened two special trains between Zhalainuo'er, Manzhouli, and Hailar to transport participants. Various Northeast organizations and institutions also sent personnel to participate. The ceremony was quite grand. Commander Wan specially sent the Chief of the Police Department, Jing Fang, and the Councilor, Du Hongnian, as representatives of the military and political departments, and carried two copies of Commander Wan's memorial text, which were read temporarily. One was a memorial text for the martyrs of the Lubin battlefield, and the other was a memorial text for the martyrs of the Zhalainuo'er battlefield. When the ceremony was held, the atmosphere was extremely solemn. The number of participants was very large. The local merchants and people, and the soldiers who participated in the war, were particularly saddened and indignant. Furthermore, the commander of the 17th Brigade of the Northeast Army Infantry stationed in the province, Yu Zhaolin, personally led all the officers of the brigade, as well as soldiers from various regiments and companies in the province (representatives from the 14th and 6th Regiments of the outer defense also participated in the memorial service), to the Martyrs' Shrine in Longsha Park to publicly commemorate the fallen soldiers who died in the defense against Russia. The atmosphere was solemn, and eulogies and memorial texts were written, with extremely tragic words and meanings.

Moreover, after the commander of the 17th Brigade of Heilongjiang, Han Guangdi, loyally died in the battle, the Northeast Political Affairs Committee had already investigated and compensated the case. Now, according to Han's wife, Ji Jufang, the family is in difficulty, and the children are orphans. All the original compensation fees can only make ends meet, and the public funds for burial have not yet been settled. She requested that a way be found. The committee then gave another 30,000 yuan. It is said that the funeral expenses are shared by Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Harbin, with Liaoning and Heilongjiang each paying 10,000 yuan, Jilin 7,000 yuan, and Harbin Special Region 3,000 yuan, and they have already been distributed separately. (18th)

The Four-Route Vehicle Clearing Conference Concludes

Agreed on the General Outline of the Clearing

Xuzhou Dispatch: The Four-Route Vehicle Clearing Conference of Jinpu, Jiaoji, Longhai, and Pinghan Railways, which has been recorded in yesterday's letter, was held on the 24th for the closing ceremony. The focus of the discussions was on the Jinpu and Longhai railways. The agreement on the methods for clearing vehicles on these two railways states: "From 0:00 on February 23rd of this year to 24:00 on November 15th, according to the tonnage, car number, railway distinction, etc., listed in the signed vouchers and account books of both parties, the original locomotives and vehicles of each railway during the period shall be jointly checked and cleared by personnel from both railways, and the surplus shall be calculated and returned separately. The handling situation shall be reported to the ministry for record."

However, the Jinpu Railway representative made two statements regarding this case: (1) If any problems occur in the above-mentioned methods, personnel from Jinpu and Longhai should be sent to jointly investigate and clarify them. The number of vehicles originally owned by each railway from 0:00 on February 23rd and the number of vehicles owned by each railway as of 24:00 on November 15th shall be used as references for the exchange. (2) The above resolution, which includes the phrase "the number of vehicles originally owned by each railway from 0:00 on February 23rd," shall not apply to the locomotives and vehicles transported by Jinpu Railway across the border during the military transportation of Commander He to defeat Feng Shi, and the locomotives and vehicles taken across the border by Shi Yousan. All the locomotives and vehicles transported across the border still belong to the Jinpu Railway.

The Longhai Railway representative also made an equivalent statement: "The Longhai Railway solemnly declares and requests to reserve the statement to the Jinpu Railway representative. This statement of reservation is only the opinion of the Jinpu Railway. This opinion, Jinpu Railway has orally stated that the resolution on the clearing of vehicles between Jinpu and Longhai Railways, which was resolved from 0:00 on February 23rd of this year to 24:00 on November 15th, according to the signed vouchers and account books of both parties, listing tonnage, number, car number, railway distinction, etc., is absolutely not involved, in order to comply with the Ministry's order to clear accounts from February 23rd, 19th year.

In short, the point of contention between the Jinpu and Longhai Railways lies in this. The two railways will send personnel to Xuzhou to calculate the accounts together. The Jiaoji and Pinghan railways will also follow this rule. However, the Jiaoji and Jinpu railways are directly related, and the accounts will be calculated together in Jinan after the meeting. The Pinghan and Longhai railways are directly related, and the accounts will be calculated together in Zhengzhou after the meeting.

With the general outline determined, the conference held a closing ceremony on the morning of the 24th. The representatives of the Ministry of Railways, the representatives of various railways, and Qian Zongze, etc., all gave speeches. Today (25th), the representatives of the Ministry of Railways, Xu Fuyin, Li Yue, Tang Dehua, etc., all returned to Beijing to report to the ministry. The representatives of various railways also left Xuzhou and returned to their respective railways to report. It is understood that during this four-route conference, Longhai's opinion advocated clearing accounts only for the military transportation period this time, without counting old debts. Jinpu's opinion was that there were many vehicles lost in the past, and the accounts should be cleared and the vehicles returned from the beginning. According to the result of mutual calculation by Longhai during the military transportation period, Jinpu still owed Longhai vehicles. According to Jinpu Railway's statistics, it still needs to claim ten locomotives and twenty trains of vehicles from Longhai. (25th)

The Great Fire in Hangzhou

Losses Amount to Approximately 400,000 Yuan

Two Firefighters Injured

Hangzhou Dispatch: At 10:50 pm on the 24th, a fire broke out in front of the Tongchunfang Haierxiang Elementary School in this city, causing a major fire. It was not extinguished until after 1:00 am on the 25th. This area is full of well-established shops, so although 40 buildings were burned down, including 27 shops, the losses have already exceeded 400,000 yuan. The responsible Fifth Precinct of the Second District has already submitted a report to the Provincial Public Security Bureau for record, including the cause of the fire and the situation of the fire, the names of the affected shops and the estimated losses. When the fire broke out, the Chishuntai Shoe Store in Tongchunfang took the opportunity to set fire. The same is true for the Tongchang Hardware Store where the fire began. The owners of both stores have been summoned for questioning. The situation at the time is recorded below:

At nearly 11 o'clock on the night of the 24th, there was still business in the area, and various teahouses were still telling stories. The Tongchang Hardware Store in Haierxiang suddenly caught fire. At the same time, the Chishuntai Shoe Store in Tongchunfang also caught fire. After about a quarter of an hour, the fire brigade and various charitable firefighting teams had arrived. At this time, electricity was falling like rain, making it difficult for rescuers to get close. A firefighter from the Second Squad of the Fire Brigade, Li Baixi from Hunan, was electrocuted and fell when he used iron pliers to demolish the house at the Fuxingyuan Teahouse, and his injuries were very serious. At the same time, a firefighter from the Qinghe Charitable Firefighting Team, A Long, was also injured in a fall, but his injuries were minor. The fire was extinguished after 1:00 am on the morning of the 25th. The owner of the Tongchang Hardware Store, Chen Baoxing, where the fire started, and the owner of the Chishuntai Shoe Store, Chi Agui, who took the opportunity to set fire, were both detained by the responsible Fifth Precinct of the Second District. A donkey from the Luyixing Tofu Store ran out when it saw the fire and was tripped by a power line in Haierxiang, causing it to be electrocuted and die.

In total, seven buildings in Tongchunfang were burned down, including four shops; sixteen buildings in Haierxiang were burned down, including ten shops; seventeen buildings in front of the elementary school were burned down, including thirteen shops. From Xinhua Hotel in the east, Zhang Tongtai Pharmacy in the south, Huanlezhai Candy Store in the west, to Chengtai Shaoxing Hotel in the north, a total of 40 door numbers were burned down, including 27 shops, with losses of more than 400,000 yuan, which can be said to be a great disaster. As for the affected households, they were Fuyu Grocery Store, Tongchang Hardware Store, Xinchang Meat Store, Fuxingyuan Teahouse, Yuanxingxiang Mill, Shunchangzhai Pastry Store, Shan Nan'an Hotel, Mingyan Barber Shop, Zhang Qingtai Grocery Store, Luyixing Tofu Store in Haierxiang; Shengchang Meat Store, Yichang Mutton Store, Liu Juchun Tofu Store, Dayouheng Preserved Meat Store, He Shuntai Tofu Store, Yuanmao Meat Store, Wanlong Egg Store, Guangren Pickles, Houchang Tobacco Store, Xiexing Mutton Store, Pan Shuntai Cooper Shop, Sun Juxing Foil Shop in front of the elementary school; Yongchun Soy Sauce Duck Shop, Ruital Cloth Shop, Yuantai Pickles, Wanxiang Dried Goods Shop in Tongchunfang. In addition, the Yi Yuan Pawnshop and Zhou Defeng Tea and Paint Shop in Tangqi were affected by a fire left by a Shaoxing fisherman who was cooking late at night around 10 p.m. on the 25th. The fire was extinguished through the efforts of the charitable fire brigades and the Bangpu water truck of the Chongyu Silk Factory. One thousand boxes of white chrysanthemums and other goods stored in the shop were burned to the ground, with losses of more than 100,000 yuan. At the time, the patrol team of the Public Security Bureau and the security regiment arrived to suppress the fire, and no accidents occurred. Afterwards, the shop manager and the Shaoxing fisherman were taken to the bureau for questioning.

Director Zhu Leaves Songjiang for Huaiyin: Zhu Huanbo, the director of the local Public Security Bureau, has served for half a year, rectifying the police affairs and making unremitting efforts, with remarkable achievements. He was previously ordered by the province to be transferred to Huaiyin. Local people telegraphed the province to retain him, but the result was unsuccessful. Zhu took a car to leave Songjiang today. Representatives from various institutions such as the County Party Department, the County Government, and the County Chamber of Commerce, as well as gentry, went to the station to see him off.

Appointment of Agricultural Association Reorganization Committee Members: The local people's organizations in this county have been reorganized by the County Reorganization Committee and are now ready. The number of members of the Farmers' Association Reorganization Committee is set at three. The Provincial Party Department has appointed Cai Yannong, Zhang Dehua, and Yao Linjiang to serve. Once the preparations are in place, work can begin.

Shanyang Communists Transferred to the Court: Pan Baozhong, the captain of the Fourth Brigade of the Anti-Smuggling Bureau of Jiangsu Province, previously discovered that Li Er Tu's Zhou family straw house near Shanyang had repeatedly held secret meetings, plotting wrongdoing. A communist named Qi A'er was seized and sent to the county government for interrogation. However, the suspect's confession was cunning, so County Chief Jin ordered the section to examine the case file and send it to the county court for handling.

Birthday Gift Used for Bridge Construction Expenses: The newly built Xibaidu Bridge in the western suburbs and the rebuilt Xiunan Bridge are large and costly projects. Although the gentlemen in charge have earnestly raised donations, they are still short of more than 1,000 yuan. It is now heard that the mother of Lei Junyao, Junyan, and Jun Cui, Mrs. Sun, will celebrate her 80th birthday on October 22nd of the lunar calendar, and plans to use the birthday banquet to cover the bridge construction expenses. It is now known that various groups such as the Education Bureau and the Bridge Construction Committee have converted the birthday gifts into cash to assist in the good deed.

Suzhou

The granary association purchased 70,000 shi of grain. The Wu County Granary Association continues to handle the "stabilized price grain" as before. Having sold two-thirds of the stored grain, only a little over 30,000 shi remain. Therefore, they plan to purchase grain to fill the granaries and have dispatched a special representative to Wuxi to purchase 70,000 shi of new grain. At five yuan per shi, the total cost is 350,000 yuan. This will be covered by 231,000 yuan in existing funds in the granary, 68,000 yuan in famine relief funds, and the remaining shortage will be made up from the land rent revenue of the 19th year [of the Republic].

The construction of Xuanmiao Temple faces new problems. The issue of demolition versus preservation of Suzhou's Xuanmiao Temple has been debated by the "preservation of antiquity" and "preservation of commerce" factions for half a year. The Executive Yuan, based on the plans proposed by the Jiangsu Construction Bureau, has already begun demolition, which can be considered to be nearing its conclusion. After the screen wall is demolished, over a hundred commercial buildings are planned to be built on the site to house various businesses. However, because the land is public property, a major question is whether the construction and rent collection should be managed by the abbot of Xuanmiao Temple or by the merchants themselves. Now, a local resident, Wang Zhaojie, has specifically petitioned the county government, stating that after the Executive Yuan's demolition order, unscrupulous merchants and evil Taoists have been active, organizing real estate companies and manipulating real estate prices, causing panic among small and medium-sized tenants and turning it into a tool for private enrichment. He requests that, following the precedent of the preservation of the Baosheng Temple in Jiaozhi, a Xuanmiao Temple Construction Committee be organized within the shortest possible time to prevent manipulation, or that the matter be submitted to the County Administrative Council for public decision.

The burden of grain transport is generally reduced by five percent. The Wu County autumn land survey and grain transport quota, previously discussed in a meeting convened by the County Bureau Chief, was submitted to the Finance Bureau at 93%. The Finance Bureau rejected the proposal, and after reconsideration, a general reduction of five percent was implemented, resulting in an effective rate of 95%, and was submitted to the Finance Bureau for approval. Yesterday, approval was received.

Resolutions of the County Administrative Council Meeting. The County Government held its 86th County Administrative Council meeting yesterday, resolving the following: (1) Regarding the case of changing the width of streets in the urban area based on the Construction Bureau's order, it was resolved to refer to the width dimensions approved by the former Municipal Public Works Bureau for handling and reply to the Construction Bureau for review. (2) Regarding the Education Bureau's severely insufficient budget and the proposal to trial a residential donation in prosperous towns and a flower and tree donation, it was resolved to postpone the residential donation and to collect the flower and tree donation.

Measures to prevent refugees from moving south. The heads of various autonomous regions in Wu County report that refugees are constantly moving south. Although the provincial authorities have explicitly ordered a halt, refugees from Suzhou, Songjiang, Changzhou, and Taicang counties continue to wander around, disturbing the people. Therefore, specific measures have been drafted and submitted to the county government for forwarding to the provincial authorities for circulation to all counties for compliance. The measures are: (1) If refugees arrive, regardless of the number, the township head will report to the district office and escort them to the city to await deportation back to their place of origin. (2) The county government of the original place of origin will restrain them from leaving again. (3) Those who resist will be punished. (4) Any looting will be punished as banditry.

Nanhui

A student strike occurred in the county. The Zhoupu Town County Junior High School formerly had a normal school program to train primary school teachers. Historically, the fees for these students were only half price to provide support for impoverished students, but since Yang Binru took over as head of the Education Bureau, the precedent of charging half fees was eliminated. The students in that program were no longer able to pay after the elimination of the benefit, and repeatedly petitioned the Education Bureau, but Director Yang insisted that it must be done, so it was difficult to achieve their goals. Therefore, the students had a lot of complaints about the Education Bureau. In this semester, Feng Guozhen took office as the school principal, but his measures were inappropriate, resulting in the students beginning a strike for some reason from the day before yesterday. Although teachers and staff tried to persuade them repeatedly, it was ineffective. The Education Bureau then appointed Chen Shixian to go to persuade them, but the students' attitude was firm, stating that they were unwilling to resume classes until a practical solution was found, so they are still on strike and a solution is difficult to find.

Wuxi

False accusations of fraud were presented to the county. Long Yunzhang, a member of the China National Road Association and a resident of Wuxi, had a dispute with his friend Huang Cangyu over book and newspaper expenses. The day before yesterday, he presented a complaint to the county government, accusing Huang Cangyu of three counts of illegal conduct: (1) Huang Cangyu forged official documents of the General Association and impersonated Chen Jun, the deputy director of the Book and Newspaper Department; (2) When Long Yunzhang was critically ill, Huang Cangyu took the opportunity to defraud him of money; (3) Huang Cangyu secretly suppressed subscription orders and delayed reporting them, causing subscribers to urge delivery, not only damaging the reputation of Long Yunzhang and others, but also affecting the credibility of the General Association. After receiving the complaint, the county government ordered Liang, the investigating judge, to summon both parties for interrogation yesterday afternoon around 4:00 PM. Huang Cangyu denied all the charges made by Long, and his words were evasive. After the interrogation, Huang Cangyu was ordered to be detained, but after Huang repeatedly begged, he was allowed to be released on bail. Long Yunzhang was ordered to return to await further interrogation.

Three more people were released in the kidnapping case. In Dengjiawan and Xiaoqiaotou, two towns bordering Jingyun and Taibo in the county, five families were robbed and seven people were kidnapped by bandits last month. The bandits released Ling Ren Da and Ling Bao Xian first, while demanding a ransom of 200,000 yuan for the remaining five people. Most recently, fourteen male and female bandits were arrested in Shanghai by the Shanghai Police Department and the local water police squad leader. The kidnapped victims were hidden elsewhere. It has been learned that the bandits, seeing that the official authorities were tightening their search and that the families of the victims were late in coming to redeem them, released three more victims yesterday, ordering them to quickly return to Wuxi to raise 12,000 yuan to redeem the rest at a certain location. It is said that the relatives of the remaining two unreleased victims have already gone to Shanghai overnight to find a solution.

Strictly deal with the sale of inferior seeds and the forging of documents. Yuan Hanchen and Zhou Meichun, Wang Xuchu (originally named Wang Meigen), residents of Nanqiao Town in the Third District (Yangming Township), sold a large batch of inferior Japanese autumn silkworm eggs in the Sushu Bridge area of Jiangyin County and forged documents from the Sericulture Control Office of the Department of Agriculture and Mines to deceive the villagers. After the matter was exposed, Yuan and others paid 300 yuan to have someone buy back the forged documents and destroy the evidence. This was discovered by He Yushu, Director of the Department of Agriculture and Mines, who sent technician Bao Chao to Wuxi for a secret investigation, which confirmed the facts. The main culprit was Wang Xuchu, who now operates the Hongren Silk Company in Changkang Lane on the road as a sales organization. Yuan Hanchen and Zhou Meichun were partners and provided assistance. Technician Bao reported the investigation to the province. After receiving the report, Director He considered that Wang Xuchu was selling inferior seeds, forging documents, and even daring to bribe officials to destroy evidence, which was extremely illegal. Yesterday, he specifically instructed the local county government to send police to arrest Wang Xuchu, Yuan Hanchen, Zhou Meichun, and others for strict handling. County Chief Pan has already complied with the order.

Telegraphing to request postponement of the issuance of Jiangsu Provincial Construction Bonds. Jiangsu Province is issuing construction bonds, with the first tranche amounting to 4 million yuan. Wuxi and Wu County have each been assigned 200,000 yuan. Now, the Suzhou business community has telegraphed the provincial authorities requesting a postponement to alleviate the people's burden. Yesterday, the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce also sent telegrams to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and the Department of Finance and the Department of Construction, stating that the market was declining and that merchants and residents could not afford it, requesting a temporary postponement to alleviate the suffering of the people of Jiangsu.

Collective discussion on protecting the Wuxi-Liyang shipping route. The Wuxi Shipping Association previously received letters from various shipping companies stating that the Wuxi-Liyi and Wuxi-Yixing routes have been repeatedly robbed. With the winter season approaching, the navigation of ships is especially important. It was agreed with the Chamber of Commerce to invite the chairmen of the Chambers of Commerce of Liyang, Yixing, and Wujin counties, as well as leaders from the banking and currency industries in the four counties, to a meeting in Wuxi. The chairmen of the Chambers of Commerce of those counties, representatives from the banking and currency industries, as well as government and police officials, arrived in Wuxi one after another yesterday (the 26th). That evening, the Wuxi Chamber of Commerce and Shipping Association hosted a dinner to welcome them. It is planned to hold a meeting today to discuss and request that both land and water police accompany the ships for protection.

Suspect in Kidnapping Arrested. Zhu prepared the money and transferred it to two friends, Cai Si and Guo Zhaoyuan, to go on his behalf, and they successfully brought the child back. Zhu Songlin has heard that Cai and Guo were also involved in the kidnapping of his son, so he reported it to the police. Changzhou

Notorious Bandit Yang Maosheng Arrested. Yang Maosheng, a notorious bandit near Panxu Town in Wujin County, recently, due to strict searches in the countryside, sneaked into the city on the 25th. The Public Security Bureau's Detective Team found out about this and was led by Deputy Captain Tang Hongming to take a detective and an informant to the Public Entertainment Place in the Old Government Temple and arrested the bandit. He was taken to the team for interrogation, and he confessed that he had kidnapped Ge Rongfa, the twelve-year-old son of Ge Qing, the village chief of Shangcheng Village in Fucheng Township, District One. It was also found that the bandit had several gunshot wounds on his left knee that had not healed. After the interrogation, he was transferred to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

A Robbery Occurred Near Jiaoxi. Bandit Leader Executed. Ningbo

Verdict in the Prosecutor's Fraud Case. Yang Hongjun, the former chief prosecutor of the Yuyao County Court, was accused of defrauding Shang Cheng by claiming to be repairing the court and subsidizing the expenses of the clerks. It has now been learned that the case was heard by the Criminal Court on the 21st of this month. After the debate ended, Yang Hongjun was sentenced to six months in prison and fined 300 yuan for attempting to illegally obtain the property of a third party by intimidating others to deliver their own property. The accomplice in the case, Wang Zaichen, was sentenced to three months in prison and fined 200 yuan.

Sea and Land Bandits Like Hair (1) The Yongping warship of the Zhenhai Water Police Bureau sailed to Nanzhai Mountain in the Shibu waters the day before yesterday and suddenly encountered several pirate ships. The captain of the ship, Xing Guoluan, directed the water police to pursue and arrest fourteen pirates, seized ten rifles and two pistols, and rescued two ships in distress and fifty-four refugees. (2) Yesterday was the day for the Shuishunfeng family on Zhongguan Road in Zhenhai Dongguan to engage their son, and it was very extravagant. At night, many bandits came to the Shuishunfeng family to rob them, stealing jewelry, clothes, cash, etc., causing a loss of about 200 yuan, and injuring his wife with a knife. (3) The banditry in the Shanyuan District of Fenghua is rampant. In the past, they would only kidnap and rob at night, but now they loot in broad daylight. The day before yesterday, Chen Zhufeng and Chen Shou from Jiukeng in that district were kidnapped again. Hangzhou

The Department of Finance Rectifies Various Taxes. The Department of Finance yesterday planned to actively and thoroughly rectify tax revenue. It specifically instructed all counties to strictly prohibit the bad practice of local organizations and various trade guilds applying for and exchanging guild licenses in the future, and not to act out of favoritism. It also sent personnel to various districts to conduct a thorough investigation, compile a register of guild licenses to avoid confusion. Old and new contracts that are not taxed will be strictly inspected when collecting grain from taxpayers. If the contract has not been taxed, they will be ordered to pay taxes. As for the tax collectors, they should first submit for verification before collecting taxes to eliminate malpractices.

Education News

Important News

Asian Education Conference

To Be Held in India on December 26

The Asian Education Conference is part of the World Education Conference. This session was initiated by the All India Federation of Teachers, which resolved to hold it in Benares, India, from December 26 to 30 of this year. The main topics of discussion are: (1) Physical education, (2) Illiteracy, (3) Adult education, (4) Libraries, (5) Preschool education, (6) Rural education, (7) Moral and religious education, (8) Parental cooperation, (9) Educational associations, (10) Teacher training, (11) Elementary education, (12) Secondary education, (13) Higher education, (14) Women's education. It is reported that the Federation has formally sent a letter to Dr. Liu Zhanen, the Chinese representative who attended the World Education Conference in Geneva last year, inviting him to attend and hoping that China will send more representatives. It is learned that Dr. Liu cannot attend due to his duties at Shanghai University. However, those in the domestic education community who are willing to accept the invitation can contact Dr. Liu.

Troubles Regarding Studies in Japan

The Ministry of Education Has Issued Instructions

Since Jiang Qi left his position as supervisor of students studying in Japan, Luo Yiqun, the Guangdong student affairs manager in Japan, temporarily replaced him for three months. Subsequently, the Ministry of Education appointed Wang Keren to take over. It has been eight months since he took office. Because of his many inappropriate actions in handling student affairs, the current dispute has arisen. The Ministry of Education has now appointed Liu Suichang to succeed him in this important role. However, a major case is still unresolved. Yesterday, it was heard that student affairs managers from various provinces in Japan had issued a "Letter to Fellow Students Studying in Japan." At the same time, it was learned that Wang Keren had accused the student affairs managers from various provinces in Japan at the Tokyo branch, wanting to charge them with the crime of being reactionary. The contents of the "Letter to Fellow Students Studying in Japan" are recorded below to show one aspect of the student affairs in Japan.

Letter from Student Affairs Managers of Various Provinces in Japan to Fellow Students Studying in Japan:

To our fellow students, the supervisor of students studying in Japan bears the heavy trust of the nation and serves as a role model for the students. The position is honorable and the responsibility is heavy, and he is closely related to the student affairs managers of various provinces in Japan, as they are all personnel in charge of student affairs in Japan. If the supervisor's office handles student affairs well, the student affairs offices of various provinces in Japan will follow and progress together, and all will benefit from it. Otherwise, they will bear the responsibility and be punished together. Honor and disgrace are related, so how can we sit idly by? Remembering that after Jiang Qi's corruption case was discovered, we and others had to file a complaint according to the law for the sake of the nation's reputation, to uphold justice and maintain discipline. The truth of this matter is hopefully understood. Anyone with a conscience should not blame us for meddling. Since Jiang Qi left office, the Ministry of Education appointed Wang Keren to take over this heavy responsibility. At the beginning of his tenure, all Chinese people studying in Japan hoped that he would be honest and upright, wash away past mistakes, and fulfill their earnest expectations. Unexpectedly, since taking office, he has been perfunctory in everything and concealed everything. Fellow students are nearby, and some have heard, some have seen, and some have even experienced it personally. For the sake of the future of student affairs, we and others had to submit our suspicions to the Ministry of Education. We know that unfortunately, in these troubled times, not speaking is a dereliction of duty, and speaking too much is careless. Those who do not know may think that we and others have already accused Jiang in the past, and now we are squeezing Wang out. They may think we have wild ambitions and want to do something. However, appeasement can lead to favor, and revolution can endanger oneself. Although we are foolish, how can we not know this? Moreover, being in a low position, we do not want to meddle in minor matters to show caution. However, because personal corruption has disgraced the nation, and because the supervisor's dereliction of duty has hindered student affairs, if we and others seek our own safety and remain silent, how can we face the Party and the nation, and how can we speak to our fellow students? Therefore, upholding the fearless spirit of the Premier, we eradicate corruption and follow the great principles of the National Government's political tutelage, fulfilling our duties. This heart will not die, and we will do what is right. We can be confident that there is absolutely no motive of power involved. Our fellow students, purify your minds and be fair in your hearts. Right and wrong will be judged by all. We are still afraid of rumors spreading and the truth being difficult to discern. Therefore, we are attaching the petition to the Ministry of Education. Whether you know or blame us, it is up to you.

Petition from Zhang Fengqian, Luo Yiqun, and Other Student Affairs Managers of Various Provinces to the Ministry of Education Regarding Matters for Inquiry:

We believe that student affairs in Japan are of utmost importance to the nation's cultural future. Therefore, the Ministry appointed a supervisor to take charge of this special duty. The supervisor's morality, learning, every move, the model for the students, and the reputation of the country are all tied to this. We deeply regret the past and feel deeply disturbed. Being in this situation, how can we remain silent? We are compelled to present the following points to the Ministry of Education and ask for your review and instructions to dispel public doubts and benefit student affairs:

(1) We have investigated that Jiang Qi, the former supervisor of students studying in Japan, was corrupt and disgraced the nation. The Ministry has already investigated and confirmed this. It has been more than half a year, but we have not seen a clear order for punishment. The public is panicked and the truth is unclear. What is the final outcome? We ask for instructions to dispel public doubts.

(2) Since Jiang Qi left office, the position of supervisor of students studying in Japan was temporarily filled by Yiqun for three months. The Ministry appointed Wang Keren to take over this heavy responsibility. At the beginning of his tenure, all Chinese people studying in Japan hoped that he would work hard for the public and correct past mistakes, so that the old stains could be washed away and student affairs could be rectified. However, Supervisor Wang's words and actions contradict each other, and he is perfunctory in everything. He is particularly secretive about finances. In recent years, due to the country's many troubles, tuition fees from various provinces have not been remitted on time, and the Japanese yen has soared, making it especially difficult for self-funded students to maintain their livelihoods. If no assistance is provided, then the students will not only have no means to study, but also no means to live. Therefore, the student affairs meeting on June 24 made a resolution to help struggling students. Afterwards, there was no news. Unexpectedly, on August 28, Yiqun, through an introduction from the embassy regarding the Tokyo Overseas Chinese Elementary School, went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to meet with Ping Shang Zhen Er, the director of cultural affairs, and talked about the recent plight of students studying in Japan. Ping Shang said that the ministry had submitted 5,000 Japanese yen to the Japan-China Society to be transferred to the supervisor's office for the purpose of helping poor students. Upon hearing this, we were shocked and thought that since there was this earmarked fund, it could be used for flexible assistance. Why had Supervisor Wang not mentioned a word about it for two months, allowing the students studying in Japan to wander and be displaced? It was not until the student affairs meeting on September 16 that we asked about this matter. Supervisor Wang said that Deng Tianming, the Jiangxi manager, had borrowed 3,000 yen, Cai Dingxun, the Hunan manager, had borrowed 1,200 yen, and the supervisor's office had used 800 yen. He claimed not to know the source of this fund, only saying that it was borrowed from the Japan-China Society. Finally, he said that the supervisor's office had also submitted 2,000 Japanese yen for assistance. However, this matter was unheard of. Moreover, he used Jiang Qi's old tricks. The next day, in the afternoon, he brought Zhang Menglin, the director of student affairs, and the day before yesterday, Lianyi Trading Company, Commercial Press, and Da Lande went to the Ministry of Cultural Affairs to ask us to confront him face to face. After we arrived at the ministry, Ping Shang repeatedly asked for understanding and said, "This fund was entrusted by several ministries to the Japan-China Society to be transferred to the supervisor's office to handle everything, considering the difficult situation of students studying in Japan. Although this fund has not been formally disbursed, when the loan period expires and no one returns it, it will be allocated again." His words were tactful, but his intentions were the same. After we questioned him, Ping Shang could not justify himself. It was a messy account that still left people unaware of the truth. As a high-ranking official appointed by the government, how could he confront a subordinate in front of foreigners? It was extremely shameful. At that time, we repeatedly told him this in Chinese, but Supervisor Wang lowered his head and said nothing, feeling deeply guilty. We believe that helping students should be done in a righteous and open manner. Why did Supervisor Wang keep it secret? We suspect that there may be something he cannot tell people. Has the Ministry approved and ordered the borrowing of foreign funds to assist students? We ask for instructions to dispel public doubts.

(3) At the student affairs meeting on September 30, Supervisor Wang suddenly claimed that he had used 5,000 Japanese yen of public funds, which had been approved by the Ministry, to help poor students. Regardless of whether he initially said 2,000 yen and then 5,000 yen, his words contradicted each other. Since there was this earmarked fund, why had the legally required student affairs meeting not discussed the method of disbursement? Moreover, after two months, not only had the managers not heard of any students benefiting, but he had also taken 800 yen from the relief fund provided by the Japanese side for other purposes. The inside story of this matter still leaves people clueless. Has this relief fund been approved and how has it been distributed? We ask for instructions to dispel public doubts.

(4) Openness in finances has long been mandated. Following Jiang Qi's mistakes, it is especially important to be open and honest to show integrity and correct bad policies. However, since Supervisor Wang took office, more than half a year has passed, and he has not followed the National Government's order (Directive No. 370) to implement financial transparency. Although we have questioned him, he has evasively said that it is inconvenient in many ways. We do not know what is inconvenient and whether there is a need to comply with government laws and regulations. We ask for instructions to dispel public doubts.

(5) Since Supervisor Wang took office, his frugality in handling affairs has been commendable. Although expenses have increased to 2,000 Japanese yen per month (according to Wang himself), he has still made every effort to reduce staff and cut costs. Recently, we heard that Dai Yuanyou, the director of general affairs, has changed his name to Liangmo and has been arranged to receive a Central Boxer Indemnity scholarship. Regardless of whether his staff reduction and cost-cutting measures are for public or private purposes, does a government official have the qualifications to receive a Boxer Indemnity scholarship concurrently? Are students who have not formally studied in a school eligible to receive a Boxer Indemnity scholarship? Is there a special purpose for changing his name? Have all these matters been submitted to the Ministry for approval? Why is this different from the previous case where Jin Muyin, a former staff member, was not allowed to receive a Boxer Indemnity scholarship concurrently? We ask for instructions to dispel public doubts.

(6) In addition to Dai Liangmo being arranged to receive a Central Boxer Indemnity scholarship, two other names have been added to the list: Fu Shisi, a preparatory student at the Tokyo Women's Medical College, and Han Jingyuan, an auditor at Waseda University. These students have shallow academic qualifications and, according to the regulations, should not be arranged to receive scholarships out of order. What is the basis for Supervisor Wang's exceptional treatment? What is the reason? Has this matter been submitted to the Ministry for approval? We ask for instructions to dispel public doubts.

The above six points are all questions. We believe that managing students should be based on fairness and integrity. If one engages in private gain and fraud and keeps things secret, not only will the credibility of the organization be lost, but it will also bring shame to the nation. We managers are eager to serve the country and dare to submit this petition, hoping that the Ministry will review it, give instructions promptly to dispel public doubts and benefit student affairs. (Remainder omitted)

Ministry of Education's Instructions:

According to the petition submitted by Zhang Fengqian and other student affairs managers of students studying in Japan, requesting instructions from the Ministry regarding six matters related to student affairs in Japan, except for the Jiang case, which the Ministry is currently investigating in detail, Dai Yuanyou has been ordered to be dismissed from his position and his Boxer Indemnity scholarship has been revoked. Han Jingyuan's qualifications for being selected for a Central Boxer Indemnity scholarship were originally unqualified. Because the case had been determined earlier, it was temporarily approved. After further investigation, it was found that there were as many as 18 people who did not meet the requirements for continuing the Boxer Indemnity scholarship, so we had to handle it strictly. The student Han Jingyuan's Boxer Indemnity scholarship should be cancelled uniformly to show fairness. As for the other claims that the office has taken 5,000 Japanese yen in subsidies from the Japanese Ministry of Cultural Affairs without authorization, and that the office's finances have not been made public, we will copy the original petition and order the office to provide a clear response. This order is issued.

Standards for Normal School Curriculum Completed

The Ministry of Education's Drafting Committee for Primary and Secondary School Curriculum Standards has completed the drafting of the normal school curriculum standards for the senior high school level and has sent them to press. It is expected to be announced and implemented within this year. The interim standards for this curriculum are structured in much the same way as other curriculum standards, but apply only to senior high school normal schools and independent normal schools at the senior high school level. The rural normal school curriculum is not included.

Location of Anti-Drug Speech for Elementary Schools

Changed to "Grand Cathay"

In addition to more than 30 schools such as Wanzhu and Xicheng, more than 10 schools, including Zhang Zhaolong of Meixi Elementary School, Fang Pengyun of Songxue Elementary School, Li Ai of Da Shiyan Elementary School, and Zhou Xiaosheng of Donghua Elementary School, registered yesterday for the Shanghai student anti-drug speech competition for elementary school students, reaching more than 50 schools in total. The number of people registered to attend the lecture is no less than 1,000. The original venue at the YMCA Auditorium was difficult to accommodate, so it was agreed with the Grand Cathay Cinema that it would be the venue for the elementary school group speech meeting from 8:00 a.m. to 1:00 p.m. on Sunday, November 30. The speech time will be changed to start at 8:30 a.m. sharp, and the speakers will be drawn at 8:15 a.m. It is heard that due to the strict time limit, a circular has been sent to the principals of all participating elementary schools in the city to notify students to arrive at the cinema near the Racecourse at 8:00 a.m. sharp. It is heard that the cinema can accommodate more than 1,300 seats. The China National Anti-Drug Association has also sent a circular to all schools that have not participated in the speech, urging them to register the number of people attending the lecture before the 28th in order to issue admission tickets, otherwise they will not be entertained. Lu Lihua, the principal of Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School, has agreed to send a large team of Girl Scouts from the school to maintain order at the venue early in the morning. The middle and high school groups will still be held at the Shanghai YMCA from 1:00 p.m. on the 29th. Yesterday, Yang Zhonghan of Daxia Affiliated High School, Chen Zhengzhang of Shanghai High School, Gao Ju of Guanghua University Affiliated High School, and Jiang Yuan of Fudan Experimental High School registered. Longmen Alumni Raise Funds to Build Statue for Yuan Guanlan

Mr. Yuan Guanlan of Baoshan dedicated his life to education and was admired by all. His fellow villagers have already held a public funeral and given him a posthumous title. His former friends and students, because Mr. Yuan founded the Longmen Normal School in the late Qing Dynasty to cultivate teachers, have made contributions to the local community. Yao Zirang, Zheng Tonghe, Mu Ouchu, Zhu Xiangwan, Lin Kanghou, Jia Jiying, Ma Qunchao and other teachers and staff of the school, as well as graduates such as Li Mofei, Gu Yinting, Di Junwu, Cheng Shisheng, Wang Dechang, Zhao Luqing, and Zhu Chunsheng, have launched a fundraising campaign at the old site of Longmen Normal School (the junior high school of Shanghai High School) to build a statue and erect a monument as a memorial. Jinan University School of Business Investigation Department Plans

To Make Great Contributions to Overseas Chinese Education and Commerce in Southeast Asia

Accepting Domestic and Foreign Commissions to Study Specific Issues

Since the establishment of the Southeast Asian Commercial Investigation Department of the School of Business of Jinan University, the work has been intense. Its plan is to: 1. Determine the scope of Southeast Asia, taking the Dutch East Indies, British Malaya, the Philippine Islands, French Indochina, Siam, and Burma as the standard for research. 2. Conduct Southeast Asian commercial statistics, with a scope including commerce, agriculture (including forestry and animal husbandry), mining, industry, fishing, finance, commodity markets, securities markets, finance, and social issues. 3. Organize the content of various statistics: 1. Sino-Southeast Asian trade statistics, 2. Southeast Asian overseas Chinese population statistics, 3. Southeast Asian important product statistics (rubber, sugar, tin, rice), 4. Sino-Southeast Asian exchange rate statistics, 5. Southeast Asian overseas Chinese remittance statistics. The department also compiles magazines and series, and accepts domestic and foreign commissions to engage in research on specific issues. If you wish to inquire, you can directly contact Liu Konggui, the secretary of the department, who holds a master's degree, or Yang Rumei, the dean of the School of Business, who holds a doctorate.

Liu Yiqi's Honors in the United States

Elected as a Member of the International Law Association

Mr. Liu Yiqi, from Jiangsu, Shanghai, is young and handsome, graduated from Chizhi University, and went to the United States to study at the University of Michigan last summer (18th year of the Republic), majoring in international public law. He obtained a master's degree in one year and immediately went to Europe to study. He has gained a lot of experience in his studies. It was recently heard that he was elected as a member of the association by the General Assembly of the American International Law Association. It is said that only a few Chinese people have been elected as members of the association. In order to further his studies and serve the Party and the country in the future, Mr. Liu is now continuing his research with famous European professors in Paris.

The First Day of the Liangjiang Chinese Sports Meet

Group Sports

The Ximen Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School and the Chinese Physical Education School held a joint sports meet at the Chinese Football Field at 2:00 p.m. yesterday. There were 20,000 guests. Thanks to the efforts of the Loujiawan Patrol Room and the Shanghai High School Boy Scouts, the order was well maintained. The meeting was scheduled to start at 2:00 p.m. After the ceremony, the performance program began. First, the bands of the two schools and all the students circled the field for a week, which was very solemn and quiet. The welcome exercises of the two schools were neat, orderly and full of spirit. The skillful movements of Chinese gymnastics, whether single, double or multiple, were all wonderful, and the word "skillful" was extremely true to its name. The Boy Scout performance was most remarkable for its watchtower spirit, which was more than 20 feet high and was completed in a few minutes, which can be described as extremely agile and skillful. The Liangjiang games, with clear singing and graceful dancing, had the essence of floating feathers. Then, the rural dance was a full expression of pastoral life. The military exercises with lying down and firing guns, the audience was refreshed, and the final pattern also won a lot of applause. The folk dance of the male students was more than just a performance, and the guests praised it. Either accompanied by piano music or assisted by military music, they complemented each other. Yesterday afternoon, the weather was fine, like a little spring in March, and the male and female guests were extremely happy. It is heard that the track and field competitions of the two schools will be held at the track and field stadium of the Chinese Sports Association on the afternoons of the 27th and 28th, but guests will not be invited, and those who like sports are free to participate. Many photographers arrived at the scene yesterday and took many photos.

Local News

General Support for Xiao and Anti-Dutch Convention

Over a Hundred Organizations and More Than a Thousand Representatives Attended

Unanimous Advocacy for Boycotting Java Company

Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, the Shanghai All Circles Support Xiao and Anti-Dutch Convention was held at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce in Tianhou Palace Bridge. More than a hundred organizations and over a thousand representatives attended. First, representatives from all circles elected city party representatives Li Zheng, Overseas Chinese Federation Chairman Xu Jigong, and representatives from various groups who initiated and convened the convention as the presidium. They then mutually elected Xu Jigong as the chairman of the presidium. After performing the rituals,

Xu Jigong reported, with Chairman Xu announcing the purpose of the meeting, briefly stating that the opinions for today's meeting are very long. Due to time constraints, he will briefly talk about the important events, which is that we have a total of three million overseas Chinese compatriots in the Dutch territories. They have suffered extreme pain, treating us like native aborigines. This is a real fact. Ms. Xiao was hired by our overseas Chinese as a teacher, but unfortunately, she was forcibly raped by the second mate of the Java Company's ship. If we promote party principles, we will also be suppressed and stopped by them. Now there is a Mr. Feng Hanyue, who was on the same ship as Ms. Xiao and knows the situation very well. We will ask him to report later. Now, let's first ask Mr. Lin Youren to report on the preparations.

Lin Youren reported, followed by preparatory member Lin Youren reporting on the preparations, briefly stating that on the one hand, it is very painful, and on the other hand, it is very comforting because the status of us Chinese in the international community is getting lower day by day. Looking back, foreign parks used to have signs prohibiting Chinese and dogs from entering, which shows that we were treated like dogs. But now we are not even as good as dogs, treating Chinese as the smallest ants. Therefore, whether at home or abroad, especially in the Dutch territories, they trample on us at will, without any consideration. We think, does everyone want to be ants and dogs, and not want to be human beings? So we are holding this meeting, which is really painful. But today, the people who came to the meeting are not here to dance or watch movies, but there are so many people, which shows that everyone wants to be human and does not want to be dogs or ants. As for Ms. Xiao's matter, everyone already knows. Ms. Xiao is a member of our nation. We must fight for the dignity of the nation and must provide assistance. The other overseas Chinese who were expelled and massacred by the Dutch cannot be counted. They believe that Chinese are the same as native aborigines. They treat native aborigines as slaves and cattle, and they also treat us as slaves and cattle. This kind of public insult is really unbearable. We Chinese have always been non-resistant, only knowing how to sigh and weep, and unable to resist with indignation. This time, if we do not assist Ms. Xiao, in the future, Chinese women will be in danger of being forcibly raped by them. All circles in Shanghai, many enthusiastic people, must have a kind of passionate expression. Everyone must know that the Netherlands is not that powerful. Their land is only over 12,000 square miles, and the population is not even twice that of Shanghai. If we work together, the people of Shanghai alone can defeat them. I hope everyone will fight to the end. After that, city party representative Li Zheng, lawyer Wu Mai, Shu Huizhen, Feng Hanyue, Liao Peizhi, and Luo Ciqi gave speeches one after another. The speeches were long, so they are omitted.

After Passing Various Proposals, Lin Youren compiled the proposals from various parties and asked the public to vote. The record is as follows: 1. Please organize a joint China Republic Support Netherlands Foreign Affairs Association from all circles. (Passed). 2. Telegraph the Central Party Department, National Government, Executive Yuan, and Ministry of Foreign Affairs to immediately telegraph the Dutch government to cancel the "China-Netherlands Consular Treaty in Dutch Territories" and its annexes. (Passed). 3. Telegraph the Central Party Department, National Government, Executive Yuan, and Ministry of Foreign Affairs to immediately negotiate with the Dutch government to amend Article 109 of the Dutch Regulations, the unequal provision of "Chinese being assimilated to native aborigines." (Passed). 4. Telegraph the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to continue negotiations to revoke the Dutch colonial parliament's resolution to increase the head tax on overseas Chinese and the supplementary collection of head tax on Chinese workers. (Passed). 5. Telegraph the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate the cancellation of the procedures for inspecting the passports of overseas Chinese entering the country and to automatically revoke the Provisional Passport Law. (Passed). 6. Please the central government to replace Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting, following the revolutionary diplomacy legacy of the Deputy Premier. (Passed, sent by the Nanyang British and Dutch Territories Expelled Overseas Chinese Promotion National Diplomacy Support Association). 7. Question the Ministry of Foreign Affairs about the reasons for stopping the boycott of Java ships. (Passed, sent by the Nanyang British and Dutch Territories Expelled Overseas Chinese Promotion National Diplomacy Support Association). 8. Telegraph the Fujian Provincial Government to stop the Xiamen Command's order to "suppress the boycott of Java ships." (Passed). 9. Telegraph domestic and foreign newspapers, news agencies, and other publications to refuse to publish Java Company advertisements and Java ship import and export news. (Passed). 10. Telegraph domestic and foreign newspapers, news agencies, and other publications to publish as much anti-Dutch news as possible and write articles to support the anti-Dutch movement. (Passed). 11. Telegraph various organizations in Xiamen, Shantou, Hong Kong, and other relevant commercial ports to jointly boycott Java ships. (Passed). 12. Telegraph the Xiamen Support Xiao Case Committee to continue organizing patrols to boycott Java ships and not be subdued by violence. All circles pledge to be the backing. (Passed). 13. Telegraph various customs clearance offices and dock associations in various ports not to declare customs or allocate goods for Java ships. (Passed). 14.
